<script>
$(function() {
    $(".hd_pops_reject").click(function() {
        var id = $(this).attr('class').split(' ');
        var ck_name = id[1];
        var exp_time = parseInt(id[2]);
        $("#"+id[1]).css("display", "none");
        set_cookie(ck_name, 1, exp_time, g5_cookie_domain);
    });
    $('.hd_pops_close').click(function() {
        var idb = $(this).attr('class').split(' ');
        $('#'+idb[1]).css('display','none');
    });
    $("#hd").css("z-index", 1000);
});
</script>

<script>
$(".btn-scrap").on('click', function() {
	var bo_table = $(this).data('table');
	var wr_id = $(this).data('id');
	var type= 'ajax';

	$.post(g5_bbs_url + '/scrap_popin_update_ajax.php',{bo_table:bo_table,wr_id:wr_id,type:type}, function(data) {
		var rst = $.parseJSON(data);
		var msg = rst['msg'].replace(/\\n/g, '\n');
		if(rst.ck == 1) {
			if (confirm(msg)) 
				window.open(g5_bbs_url+ '/scrap.php');
		} else {
			alert(msg);
		}	
	});
});
</script>							</div><!-- .at-body -->
